     9	  [/^op(?:acity)?-?(.+)$/, ([, d]) => ({ opacity: h.bracket.percent.cssvar(d) })],
    10	]

    12	const bgUrlRE = /^\[url\(.+\)\]$/
    13	const bgLengthRE = /^\[(?:length|size):.+\]$/
    14	const bgPositionRE = /^\[position:.+\]$/
    15	const bgGradientRE = /^\[(?:linear|conic|radial)-gradient\(.+\)\]$/
    16	const bgImageRE = /^\[image:.+\]$/
    17	
    18	export const bgColors: Rule<Theme>[] = [
    19	  [/^bg-(.+)$/, (...args) => {
    20	    const d = args[0][1]
    21	    if (bgUrlRE.test(d))
    22	      return { '--un-url': h.bracket(d), 'background-image': 'var(--un-url)' }
    23	    if (bgLengthRE.test(d) && h.bracketOfLength(d) != null)
    24	      return { 'background-size': h.bracketOfLength(d)!.split(' ').map(e => h.fraction.auto.px.cssvar(e) ?? e).join(' ') }
    25	    if ((isSize(d) || bgPositionRE.test(d)) && h.bracketOfPosition(d) != null)
    26	      return { 'background-position': h.bracketOfPosition(d)!.split(' ').map(e => h.position.fraction.auto.px.cssvar(e) ?? e).join(' ') }
    27	    if (bgGradientRE.test(d) || bgImageRE.test(d)) {
    28	      const s = h.bracket(d)
    29	      if (s) {
    30	        const url = s.startsWith('http') ? `url(${s})` : h.cssvar(s)
    31	        return { 'background-image': url ?? s }
    32	      }
    33	    }
    34	    return colorResolver('background-color', 'bg')(...args)
    35	  }, { autocomplete: 'bg-$colors' }],

     1	import type { CSSColorValue } from '@unocss/rule-utils'
     2	import { alphaPlaceholders, alphaPlaceholdersRE, cssColorFunctions } from '@unocss/rule-utils'
     3	
     4	export function colorOpacityToString(color: CSSColorValue) {
     5	  const alpha = color.alpha ?? 1
     6	  return (typeof alpha === 'string' && alphaPlaceholders.includes(alpha))
     7	    ? 1
     8	    : alpha
     9	}
    10	
    11	export function colorToString(color: CSSColorValue | string, alphaOverride?: string | number) {
    12	  if (typeof color === 'string')
    13	    return color.replace(alphaPlaceholdersRE, `${alphaOverride ?? 1}`)
    14	
    15	  const { components } = color
    16	  let { alpha, type } = color
    17	  alpha = alphaOverride ?? alpha
    18	  type = type.toLowerCase()
    19	
    20	  if (['hsla', 'rgba'].includes(type))
    21	    return `${type}(${components.join(', ')}${alpha == null ? '' : `, ${alpha}`})`
    22	
    23	  alpha = alpha == null ? '' : ` / ${alpha}`
    24	  if (cssColorFunctions.includes(type))
    25	    return `${type}(${components.join(' ')}${alpha})`
    26	  return `color(${type} ${components.join(' ')}${alpha})`
    27	}

     1	import type { Postprocessor } from '@unocss/core'
     2	import type { PresetWind4Options } from '..'
     3	
     4	export function important({ important: option }: PresetWind4Options): Postprocessor[] {
     5	  if (option == null || option === false)
     6	    return []
     7	
     8	  const wrapWithIs = (selector: string) => {
     9	    if (selector.startsWith(':is(') && selector.endsWith(')'))
    10	      return selector
    11	
    12	    // handle pseudo
    13	    if (selector.includes('::'))
    14	      return selector.replace(/(.*?)((?:\s\*)?::.*)/, ':is($1)$2')
    15	
    16	    return `:is(${selector})`
    17	  }
    18	
    19	  return [
    20	    option === true
    21	      ? (util) => {
    22	          // If the util is a property layer, we should not add `!important` to it
    23	          if (util.layer === 'properties')
    24	            return
    25	
    26	          util.entries.forEach((i) => {
    27	            if (i[1] != null && !String(i[1]).endsWith('!important'))
    28	              i[1] += ' !important'
    29	          })
    30	        }
    31	      : (util) => {
    32	          if (!util.selector.startsWith(option))
    33	            util.selector = `${option} ${wrapWithIs(util.selector)}`
    34	        },
    35	  ]
    36	}

    11	// #region Number Resolver
    12	export function numberResolver(size: string, defaultValue?: string | number): number | undefined {
    13	  const v = h.number(size) ?? defaultValue
    14	
    15	  if (v != null) {
    16	    let num = Number(v)
    17	    if (String(v).endsWith('%')) {
    18	      num = Number(String(v).slice(0, -1)) / 100
    19	    }
    20	
    21	    return num
    22	  }
    23	}
    24	// #endregion
    25	
    26	// #region Direction with size
    27	/**
    28	 * Provide {@link DynamicMatcher} function returning spacing definition. See spacing rules.
    29	 *
    30	 * @param propertyPrefix - Property for the css value to be created. Postfix will be appended according to direction matched.
    31	 * @see {@link directionMap}
    32	 */
    33	export function directionSize(propertyPrefix: string): DynamicMatcher<Theme> {
    34	  function parseNumberWithUnit(str: string): [number | undefined, string | undefined] {
    35	    const match = str.match(numberWithUnitRE)
    36	    if (match) {
    37	      const [, n, unit] = match
    38	      const num = Number.parseFloat(n)
    39	      if (!Number.isNaN(num))
    40	        return [num, unit]
    41	    }
    42	    return [undefined, undefined]
    43	  }
    44	
    45	  function resolveSpace(theme: Theme) {
    46	    let base: number | undefined
    47	    let unit: string | undefined
    48	
    49	    if (theme.spacing?.DEFAULT) {
    50	      const [v, u] = parseNumberWithUnit(theme.spacing.DEFAULT)
    51	      if (v != null && u != null) {
    52	        base = v
    53	        unit = u
    54	      }
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    return Object.entries(theme.spacing ?? {}).reduce((acc, [key, value]) => {
    58	      const [v, u] = parseNumberWithUnit(value)
    59	
    60	      if (v != null && u != null && u === unit) {
    61	        acc[key] = v / base!
    62	      }
    63	      else {
    64	        acc[key] = value
    65	      }
    66	
    67	      return acc
    68	    }, {} as Record<string, number | string>)
    69	  }
    70	
    71	  return (([_, direction, size]: (string | undefined)[], { theme }): CSSEntries | undefined => {
    72	    if (size != null && direction != null) {
    73	      const spaceMap = resolveSpace(theme)
    74	      let v: string | number | undefined
    75	
    76	      const isNegative = size.startsWith('-')
    77	      if (isNegative)
    78	        size = size.slice(1)
    79	
    80	      v = numberResolver(size, spaceMap[size as keyof typeof spaceMap])
    81	
    82	      if (v != null) {
    83	        if (!Number.isNaN(v)) {
    84	          themeTracking('spacing')
    85	          return directionMap[direction].map(i => [`${propertyPrefix}${i}`, `calc(var(--spacing) * ${isNegative ? '-' : ''}${v})`])
    86	        }
    87	        else {
    88	          themeTracking('spacing', size)
    89	          return directionMap[direction].map(i => [`${propertyPrefix}${i}`, isNegative ? `calc(var(--spacing-${size} * -1)` : `var(--spacing-${size})`])
    90	        }
    91	      }
    92	
    93	      v = h.bracket.cssvar.global.auto.fraction.rem(isNegative ? `-${size}` : size)
    94	
    95	      if (v != null) {
    96	        return directionMap[direction].map(i => [`${propertyPrefix}${i}`, v])
    97	      }
    98	    }
    99	  }) as DynamicMatcher<Theme>
   100	}

   105	// #region Parse color
   106	
   107	/**
   108	 * Split utility shorthand delimited by / or :
   109	 */
   110	export function splitShorthand(body: string, type: string) {
   111	  const [front, rest] = getStringComponent(body, '[', ']', ['/', ':']) ?? []
   112	
   113	  if (front != null) {
   114	    const match = (front.match(bracketTypeRe) ?? [])[1]
   115	
   116	    if (match == null || match === type)
   117	      return [front, rest]
   118	  }
   119	}
   120	
   121	/**
   122	 * Parse color string into {@link ParsedColorValue} (if possible). Color value will first be matched to theme object before parsing.
   123	 * See also color.tests.ts for more examples.
   124	 *
   125	 * @example Parseable strings:
   126	 * 'red' // From theme, if 'red' is available
   127	 * 'red-100' // From theme, plus scale
   128	 * 'red-100/20' // From theme, plus scale/opacity
   129	 * '[rgb(100 2 3)]/[var(--op)]' // Bracket with rgb color and bracket with opacity
   130	 * '[rgb(100 2 3)]/[var(--op)]/[in_oklab]' // Bracket with rgb color, bracket with opacity and bracket with interpolation method
   131	 *
   132	 * @param body - Color string to be parsed.
   133	 * @param theme - {@link Theme} object.
   134	 * @return object if string is parseable.
   135	 */
   136	export function parseColor(body: string, theme: Theme) {
   137	  let split
   138	  const [front, ...rest] = getStringComponents(body, ['/', ':'], 3) ?? []
   139	
   140	  if (front != null) {
   141	    const match = (front.match(bracketTypeRe) ?? [])[1]
   142	
   143	    if (match == null || match === 'color') {
   144	      split = [front, ...rest]
   145	    }
   146	  }
   147	
   148	  if (!split)
   149	    return
   150	
   151	  let opacity: string | undefined
   152	  let [main, opacityOrModifier, modifier] = split as [string, string | undefined, string | undefined]
   153	
   154	  if (isInterpolatedMethod(opacityOrModifier) || isInterpolatedMethod(h.bracket(opacityOrModifier ?? ''))) {
   155	    modifier = opacityOrModifier
   156	  }
   157	  else {
   158	    opacity = opacityOrModifier
   159	  }
   160	
   161	  const colors = main
   162	    .replace(/([a-z])(\d)(?![-_a-z])/g, '$1-$2')
   163	    .split(/-/g)
   164	  const [name] = colors
   165	
   166	  if (!name)
   167	    return
   168	
   169	  let parsed = parseThemeColor(theme, colors)
   170	  if (!parsed && colors.length >= 2) {
   171	    // If the last part of the color is numbers, merge the last two parts
   172	    // e.g. ['foo', 'bar', '1'] should be parsed as ['foo', 'bar1']
   173	    // try the last key is `bar1` in the theme.
   174	    const last = colors.at(-1)
   175	    const secondLast = colors.at(-2)
   176	    if (/^\d+$/.test(last!)) {
   177	      const keys = colors.slice(0, -2).concat([`${secondLast}${last}`])
   178	      parsed = parseThemeColor(theme, keys)
   179	    }
   180	  }
   181	
   182	  let { no, keys, color } = parsed ?? {}
   183	
   184	  if (!color) {
   185	    const bracket = h.bracketOfColor(main)
   186	    const bracketOrMain = bracket || main
   187	
   188	    if (h.numberWithUnit(bracketOrMain))
   189	      return
   190	
   191	    if (/^#[\da-f]+$/i.test(bracketOrMain))
   192	      color = bracketOrMain
   193	    else if (/^hex-[\da-fA-F]+$/.test(bracketOrMain))
   194	      color = `#${bracketOrMain.slice(4)}`
   195	    else if (main.startsWith('$'))
   196	      color = h.cssvar(main)
   197	
   198	    color = color || bracket
   199	  }
   200	
   201	  return {
   202	    opacity,
   203	    modifier: (modifier && h.bracket.cssvar(modifier)) || modifier,
   204	    name,
   205	    no,
   206	    color: color ?? SpecialColorKey[name as keyof typeof SpecialColorKey],
   207	    alpha: h.bracket.cssvar.percent(opacity ?? ''),
   208	    /**
   209	     * Keys means the color is from theme object.
   210	     */
   211	    keys,
   212	    get cssColor() {
   213	      return parseCssColor(this.color)
   214	    },
   215	  }
   216	}
   217	
   218	export function parseThemeColor(theme: Theme, keys: string[]) {
   219	  let color: string | undefined
   220	  let no
   221	  let key
   222	
   223	  const colorData = getThemeByKey(theme, 'colors', keys)
   224	
   225	  if (typeof colorData === 'object') {
   226	    if ('DEFAULT' in colorData) {
   227	      color = colorData.DEFAULT
   228	      no = 'DEFAULT'
   229	      key = [...keys, no]
   230	    }
   231	  }
   232	  else if (typeof colorData === 'string') {
   233	    color = colorData
   234	    key = keys
   235	    no = keys.at(-1)
   236	  }
   237	
   238	  if (!color)
   239	    return
   240	
   241	  return {
   242	    color,
   243	    no,
   244	    keys: key,
   245	  }
   246	}
   247	
   248	export function getThemeByKey(theme: Theme, themeKey: keyof Theme, keys: string[]) {
   249	  const obj = theme[themeKey]
   250	  function deepGet(current: any, path: string[]): any {
   251	    if (!current || typeof current !== 'object')
   252	      return undefined
   253	    if (path.length === 0)
   254	      return current
   255	    // First, check if the path is a flat key (e.g., foo-bar)
   256	    for (let i = path.length; i > 0; i--) {
   257	      const flatKey = path.slice(0, i).join('-')
   258	      if (flatKey in current) {
   259	        const v = current[flatKey]
   260	        if (i === path.length)
   261	          return v
   262	        // look for the rest of the path
   263	        return deepGet(v, path.slice(i))
   264	      }
   265	    }
   266	    return undefined
   267	  }
   268	  return deepGet(obj, keys)
   269	}
   270	
   271	// #endregion
   272	
   273	// #region Color Resolver
   274	
   275	export function colorCSSGenerator(
   276	  data: ReturnType<typeof parseColor>,
   277	  property: string,
   278	  varName: string,
   279	  ctx?: RuleContext<Theme>,
   280	): [CSSObject, ...CSSValueInput[]] | undefined {
   281	  if (!data)
   282	    return
   283	
   284	  const { color, keys, alpha, modifier } = data
   285	  const rawColorComment = ctx?.generator.config.envMode === 'dev' && color ? ` /* ${color} */` : ''
   286	  const css: CSSObject = {}
   287	
   288	  if (color) {
   289	    const result: [CSSObject, ...CSSValueInput[]] = [css]
   290	
   291	    if (Object.values(SpecialColorKey).includes(color)) {
   292	      css[property] = color
   293	    }
   294	    else {
   295	      const alphaKey = `--un-${varName}-opacity`
   296	      const value = keys ? generateThemeVariable('colors', keys) : color
   297	      let method = modifier ?? (keys ? 'in srgb' : 'in oklab')
   298	      if (!method.startsWith('in ') && !method.startsWith('var(')) {
   299	        method = `in ${method}`
   300	      }
   301	
   302	      css[property] = `color-mix(${method}, ${value} ${alpha ?? `var(${alphaKey})`}, transparent)${rawColorComment}`
   303	      result.push(defineProperty(alphaKey, { syntax: '<percentage>', initialValue: '100%' }))
   304	
   305	      if (keys) {
   306	        themeTracking(`colors`, keys)
   307	        if (!modifier) {
   308	          result.push({
   309	            [symbols.parent]: '@supports (color: color-mix(in lab, red, red))',
   310	            [symbols.noMerge]: true,
   311	            [symbols.shortcutsNoMerge]: true,
   312	            [property]: `color-mix(in oklab, ${value} ${alpha ?? `var(${alphaKey})`}, transparent)${rawColorComment}`,
   313	          })
   314	        }
   315	      }
   316	      if (ctx?.theme) {
   317	        detectThemeValue(color, ctx.theme)
   318	      }
   319	    }
   320	
   321	    return result
   322	  }
   323	}
   324	
   325	export function colorResolver(property: string, varName: string) {
   326	  return ([, body]: string[], ctx: RuleContext<Theme>): (CSSValueInput | string)[] | undefined => {
   327	    const data = parseColor(body ?? '', ctx.theme)
   328	    if (!data)
   329	      return
   330	
   331	    return colorCSSGenerator(data, property, varName, ctx) as (CSSValueInput | string)[]
   332	  }
   333	}
   334	
   335	// #endregion
   336	
   337	export function colorableShadows(shadows: string | string[], colorVar: string) {
   338	  const colored = []
   339	  shadows = toArray(shadows)
   340	  for (let i = 0; i < shadows.length; i++) {
   341	    // shadow values are between 3 to 6 terms including color
   342	    const components = getStringComponents(shadows[i], ' ', 6)
   343	    if (!components || components.length < 3)
   344	      return shadows
   345	
   346	    let isInset = false
   347	    const pos = components.indexOf('inset')
   348	    if (pos !== -1) {
   349	      components.splice(pos, 1)
   350	      isInset = true
   351	    }
   352	
   353	    let colorVarValue = ''
   354	    const lastComp = components.at(-1)
   355	    if (parseCssColor(components.at(0))) {
   356	      const color = parseCssColor(components.shift())
   357	      if (color)
   358	        colorVarValue = `, ${colorToString(color)}`
   359	    }
   360	    else if (parseCssColor(lastComp)) {
   361	      const color = parseCssColor(components.pop())
   362	      if (color)
   363	        colorVarValue = `, ${colorToString(color)}`
   364	    }
   365	    else if (lastComp && cssVarFnRE.test(lastComp)) {
   366	      const color = components.pop()!
   367	      colorVarValue = `, ${color}`
   368	    }
   369	
   370	    colored.push(`${isInset ? 'inset ' : ''}${components.join(' ')} var(${colorVar}${colorVarValue})`)
   371	  }
   372	
   373	  return colored
   374	}
   375	
   376	export function hasParseableColor(color: string | undefined, theme: Theme) {
   377	  return color != null && !!parseColor(color, theme)?.color
   378	}
   379	
   380	// #endregion
   381	
   382	// #region resolve breakpoints
   383	const reLetters = /[a-z]+/gi
   384	const resolvedBreakpoints = new WeakMap<any, { point: string, size: string }[]>()
   385	
   386	export function resolveBreakpoints({ theme, generator }: Readonly<VariantContext<Theme>>, key: 'breakpoint' | 'verticalBreakpoint' = 'breakpoint') {
   387	  const breakpoints: Record<string, string> | undefined = (generator?.userConfig?.theme as any)?.[key] || theme[key]
   388	
   389	  if (!breakpoints)
   390	    return undefined
   391	
   392	  if (resolvedBreakpoints.has(theme))
   393	    return resolvedBreakpoints.get(theme)
   394	
   395	  const resolved = Object.entries(breakpoints)
   396	    .sort((a, b) => Number.parseInt(a[1].replace(reLetters, '')) - Number.parseInt(b[1].replace(reLetters, '')))
   397	    .map(([point, size]) => ({ point, size }))
   398	
   399	  resolvedBreakpoints.set(theme, resolved)
   400	  return resolved
   401	}
   402	
   403	export function resolveVerticalBreakpoints(context: Readonly<VariantContext<Theme>>) {
   404	  return resolveBreakpoints(context, 'verticalBreakpoint')
   405	}
   406	// #endregion
   407	
   408	// #region Global static & defineProperty
   409	export function makeGlobalStaticRules(prefix: string, property?: string): StaticRule[] {
   410	  return globalKeywords.map(keyword => [`${prefix}-${keyword}`, { [property ?? prefix]: keyword }])
   411	}
   412	
   413	export function defineProperty(
   414	  property: string,
   415	  options: { syntax?: string, inherits?: boolean, initialValue?: unknown } = {},
   416	): CSSValueInput {
   417	  const {
   418	    syntax = '*',
   419	    inherits = false,
   420	    initialValue,
   421	  } = options
   422	
   423	  const value: CSSObjectInput = {
   424	    [symbols.shortcutsNoMerge]: true,
   425	    [symbols.noMerge]: true,
   426	    [symbols.variants]: () => [
   427	      {
   428	        parent: '',
   429	        layer: 'properties',
   430	        selector: () => `@property ${property}`,
   431	      },
   432	    ],
   433	    syntax: JSON.stringify(syntax),
   434	    inherits: inherits ? 'true' : 'false',
   435	  }
   436	  if (initialValue != null) {
   437	    value['initial-value'] = initialValue as keyof CSSObjectInput
   438	  }
   439	  propertyTracking(property, initialValue ? String(initialValue) : 'initial')
   440	  return value
   441	}
   442	// #endregion
   443	
   444	// #region Basic util functions
   445	export function isCSSMathFn(value: string | undefined) {
   446	  return value != null && cssMathFnRE.test(value)
   447	}
   448	
   449	export function isSize(str: string) {
   450	  if (str[0] === '[' && str.slice(-1) === ']')
   451	    str = str.slice(1, -1)
   452	  return cssMathFnRE.test(str) || numberWithUnitRE.test(str)
   453	}
   454	
   455	export function camelize(str: string) {
   456	  return str.replace(/-(\w)/g, (_, c) => c ? c.toUpperCase() : '')
   457	}
   458	
   459	export function hyphenate(str: string) {
   460	  return str.replace(/(?:^|\B)([A-Z])/g, '-$1').toLowerCase()
   461	}
   462	
   463	export function compressCSS(css: string, isDev = false) {
   464	  if (isDev)
   465	    return css.trim()
   466	  return css.trim().replace(/\s+/g, ' ').replace(/\/\*[\s\S]*?\*\//g, '')
   467	}
   468	// #endregion
   469

   145	    /^font-(.+)$/,

   150	      if (theme.font?.[d]) {
   151	        themeTracking('font', d)
   152	        v = generateThemeVariable('font', d)
   153	        return { 'font-family': v }
   154	      }
   155	
   156	      // Prefer theme font weight
   157	      if (theme.fontWeight?.[d]) {
   158	        themeTracking('fontWeight', d)
   159	        v = generateThemeVariable('fontWeight', d)
   160	        return { '--un-font-weight': v, 'font-weight': v }
   161	      }
   162	
   163	      // Numeric font weight (e.g. font-700)
   164	      v = h.number(d)
   165	      if (v != null) {
   166	        return { '--un-font-weight': v, 'font-weight': v }
   167	      }
   168	
   169	      // Bracketed font family (e.g. font-[family:Inter])
   170	      v = h.bracketOfFamily(d)
   171	      if (v != null && h.number(v) == null) {
   172	        v = h.cssvar(v) ?? v
   173	        return { 'font-family': v }
   174	      }
   175	
   176	      // Bracketed numeric font weight (e.g. font-[number:700])
   177	      v = h.bracketOfNumber(d)
   178	      if (v != null) {
   179	        v = h.cssvar.number(v)
   180	        return { '--un-font-weight': v, 'font-weight': v }
   181	      }
   182	
   183	      // Bracketed value that is a unknown (e.g. font-[sth])
   184	      v = h.bracket(d)
   185	      if (v != null && h.number(v) != null) {
   186	        const num = h.number(v)
   187	        return { '--un-font-weight': num, 'font-weight': num }
   188	      }
   189	
   190	      v = h.bracket.cssvar.global(d)
   191	      if (v != null) {
   192	        return { 'font-family': v }
   193	      }
   194	    },
   195	    { autocomplete: ['font-$font', 'font-$fontWeight'] },
   196	  ],

   297	
   298	function handleText([, s = 'base']: string[], { theme }: RuleContext<Theme>): CSSObject | undefined {
   299	  const split = splitShorthand(s, 'length')
   300	  if (!split)
   301	    return
   302	
   303	  const [size, leading] = split
   304	
   305	  const sizePairs = theme.text?.[size]
   306	  let lineHeight
   307	
   308	  if (leading) {
   309	    if (theme.leading?.[leading]) {
   310	      themeTracking(`leading`, leading)
   311	      lineHeight = generateThemeVariable('leading', leading)
   312	    }
   313	    else {
   314	      lineHeight = h.bracket.cssvar.global.rem(leading)
   315	    }
   316	  }
   317	
   318	  if (sizePairs) {
   319	    themeTracking(`text`, [size, 'fontSize'])
   320	    themeTracking(`text`, [size, 'lineHeight'])
   321	    if (sizePairs.letterSpacing) {
   322	      themeTracking(`text`, [size, 'letterSpacing'])
   323	    }
   324	
   325	    return {
   326	      'font-size': generateThemeVariable('text', [size, 'fontSize']),
   327	      'line-height': lineHeight ?? `var(--un-leading, ${generateThemeVariable('text', [size, 'lineHeight'])})`,
   328	      'letter-spacing': sizePairs.letterSpacing ? generateThemeVariable('text', [size, 'letterSpacing']) : undefined,
   329	    }
   330	  }
   331	
   332	  const fontSize = h.bracketOfLength.rem(size)
   333	  if (lineHeight && fontSize) {
   334	    return {
   335	      'font-size': fontSize,
   336	      'line-height': lineHeight,
   337	    }
   338	  }
   339	
   340	  return { 'font-size': h.bracketOfLength.rem(s) }
   341	}
   342	
   343	function handleSize([, s]: string[], { theme }: RuleContext<Theme>): CSSObject | undefined {
   344	  if (theme.text?.[s] != null) {
   345	    themeTracking(`text`, [s, 'fontSize'])
   346	    themeTracking(`text`, [s, 'lineHeight'])
   347	    return {
   348	      'font-size': generateThemeVariable('text', [s, 'fontSize']),
   349	      'line-height': `var(--un-leading, ${generateThemeVariable('text', [s, 'lineHeight'])})`,
   350	    }
   351	  }
   352	  else {
   353	    const d = h.bracket.cssvar.global.rem(s)
   354	    if (d)
   355	      return { 'font-size': d }
   356	  }
   357	}
   358	
   359	function handlerColorOrSize(match: RegExpMatchArray, ctx: RuleContext<Theme>): CSSObject | (CSSValueInput | string)[] | undefined {
   360	  if (isCSSMathFn(h.bracket(match[1])))
   361	    return handleSize(match, ctx)
   362	  return colorResolver('color', 'text')(match, ctx)
   363	}
   364	
   365	export function splitShorthand(body: string, type: string) {
   366	  const [front, rest] = getStringComponent(body, '[', ']', ['/', ':']) ?? []
   367	
   368	  if (front != null) {
   369	    const match = (front.match(bracketTypeRe) ?? [])[1]
   370	
   371	    if (match == null || match === type)
   372	      return [front, rest]
   373	  }
   374	}

   276	  data: ReturnType<typeof parseColor>,
   277	  property: string,
   278	  varName: string,
   279	  ctx?: RuleContext<Theme>,
   280	): [CSSObject, ...CSSValueInput[]] | undefined {
   281	  if (!data)
   282	    return
   283

   285	  const rawColorComment = ctx?.generator.config.envMode === 'dev' && color ? ` /* ${color} */` : ''
   286	  const css: CSSObject = {}
   287	
   288	  if (color) {
   289	    const result: [CSSObject, ...CSSValueInput[]] = [css]
   290	
   291	    if (Object.values(SpecialColorKey).includes(color)) {
   292	      css[property] = color
   293	    }
   294	    else {
   295	      const alphaKey = `--un-${varName}-opacity`
   296	      const value = keys ? generateThemeVariable('colors', keys) : color
   297	      let method = modifier ?? (keys ? 'in srgb' : 'in oklab')
   298	      if (!method.startsWith('in ') && !method.startsWith('var(')) {
   299	        method = `in ${method}`
   300	      }
   301	
   302	      css[property] = `color-mix(${method}, ${value} ${alpha ?? `var(${alphaKey})`}, transparent)${rawColorComment}`
   303	      result.push(defineProperty(alphaKey, { syntax: '<percentage>', initialValue: '100%' }))
   304

   310	            [symbols.noMerge]: true,
   311	            [symbols.shortcutsNoMerge]: true,

   315	      }

   326	  return ([, body]: string[], ctx: RuleContext<Theme>): (CSSValueInput | string)[] | undefined => {

     2	import type { Theme } from '../theme'
     3	import { trackedProperties } from '../utils/track'
     4	
     5	export function properties(): Preflight<Theme> | undefined {
     6	  return {
     7	    getCSS: () => {
     8	      if (trackedProperties.size > 0) {
     9	        const parent = `@supports ((-webkit-hyphens: none) and (not (margin-trim: inline))) or ((-moz-orient: inline) and (not (color:rgb(from red r g b))))`
    10	        const root = `*, ::before, ::after, ::backdrop`
    11	        const css = Array.from(trackedProperties.entries())
    12	          .map(([property, value]) => `${property}:${value};`)
    13	          .join('')
    14	
    15	        return `${parent}{${root}{${css}}}`
    16	      }

     1	import type { Postprocessor } from '@unocss/core'
     2	import type { PresetWind4Options } from '..'
     3	
     4	export function important({ important: option }: PresetWind4Options): Postprocessor[] {
     5	  if (option == null || option === false)
     6	    return []
     7	
     8	  const wrapWithIs = (selector: string) => {
     9	    if (selector.startsWith(':is(') && selector.endsWith(')'))
    10	      return selector
    11	
    12	    // handle pseudo
    13	    if (selector.includes('::'))
    14	      return selector.replace(/(.*?)((?:\s\*)?::.*)/, ':is($1)$2')
    15	
    16	    return `:is(${selector})`
    17	  }
    18	
    19	  return [
    20	    option === true
    21	      ? (util) => {
    22	          // If the util is a property layer, we should not add `!important` to it
    23	          if (util.layer === 'properties')
    24	            return
    25	
    26	          util.entries.forEach((i) => {
    27	            if (i[1] != null && !String(i[1]).endsWith('!important'))
    28	              i[1] += ' !important'
    29	          })
    30	        }
    31	      : (util) => {
    32	          if (!util.selector.startsWith(option))
    33	            util.selector = `${option} ${wrapWithIs(util.selector)}`
    34	        },
    35	  ]
    36	}
    37

Perfect! I found the issue. The problem is in the `important` postprocessor. When `important` is set to a CSS selector like `#__nuxt`, the processor wraps all utility selectors except properties that start with the important selector. However, it's incorrectly applying the important wrapper to the `@property` rule as well.

Looking at the generated CSS, we can see:
- `#__nuxt :is(@property --un-text-opacity){...}` - This is wrong! `@property` should not be inside `#__nuxt`
- The CSS property `--un-text-opacity:100%;` is correctly defined globally

The issue is that the important postprocessor doesn't distinguish between regular CSS rules and `@property` rules. The `@property` rule should not be wrapped with the important selector since it's not a regular CSS rule.

Let me examine how the `@property` rule is generated:

const { presetWind4 } = require('"'"'@unocss/preset-wind4'"'"');

async function runTest(testName, config, utility) {
  console.log(`\n🧪 ${testName}`);
  
  const uno = await createGenerator({
    presets: [presetWind4(config)]
  });

  const { css } = await uno.generate(utility);
  
  // Check if @property rules are properly located
  const propertyRules = css.match(/@property\s+[^{]+\{[^}]+\}/g) || [];
  let hasInvalidPropertyRule = false;
  
  propertyRules.forEach(rule => {
    if (rule.includes('"'"'#__nuxt'"'"')) {
      console.log('"'"'❌ Found @property rule inside #__nuxt selector:'"'"', rule);
      hasInvalidPropertyRule = true;
    }
  });
  
  if (!hasInvalidPropertyRule && propertyRules.length > 0) {
    console.log('"'"'✅ @property rules are correctly positioned'"'"');
  }
  
  // Check if CSS variables are properly defined and used
  const usesColorMix = css.includes('"'"'color-mix'"'"');
  const hasOpacityVar = css.includes('"'"'--un-text-opacity'"'"');
  const usesOpacityVar = css.includes('"'"'var(--un-text-opacity)'"'"');
  
  if (usesColorMix && hasOpacityVar && usesOpacityVar) {
    console.log('"'"'✅ CSS variables are properly defined and used'"'"');
  } else {
    console.log('"'"'❌ CSS variable issue:'"'"');
    console.log('"'"'   - Uses color-mix:'"'"', usesColorMix);
    console.log('"'"'   - Has opacity var:'"'"', hasOpacityVar);
    console.log('"'"'   - Uses opacity var:'"'"', usesOpacityVar);
  }
}

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_edge_cases.cjs --file_text 'const { createGenerator } = require('"'"'@unocss/core'"'"');
const { presetWind4 } = require('"'"'@unocss/preset-wind4'"'"');

async function checkCSSVariables(css, utility) {
  console.log(`\n🔍 Checking CSS for: ${utility}`);
  
  // Extract all @property rules
  const propertyRules = css.match(/@property\s+([^{]+)\{([^}]+)\}/g) || [];
  
  if (propertyRules.length > 0) {
    console.log('"'"'📋 Found @property rules:'"'"');
    propertyRules.forEach((rule, i) => {
      const isInsideSelector = rule.includes('"'"'#__nuxt'"'"');
      console.log(`   ${i + 1}. ${isInsideSelector ? '"'"'❌ INSIDE #__nuxt'"'"' : '"'"'✅ Correctly placed'"'"'}: ${rule.trim()}`);
    });
  } else {
    console.log('"'"'ℹ️ No @property rules found'"'"');
  }
  
  // Check variable usage
  const vars = ['"'"'--un-text-opacity'"'"', '"'"'--un-bg-opacity'"'"', '"'"'--un-border-opacity'"'"'];
  vars.forEach(varName => {
    const hasDefinition = css.includes(`${varName}:`);
    const hasUsage = css.includes(`var(${varName})`);
    
    if (hasDefinition && hasUsage) {
      console.log(`✅ ${varName}: defined and used correctly`);
    } else if (hasDefinition && !hasUsage) {
      console.log(`⚠️  ${varName}: defined but not used`);
    } else if (!hasDefinition && hasUsage) {
      console.log(`❌ ${varName}: used but NOT defined!`);
    }
  });
}

async function main() {
  console.log('"'"'🧪 Testing edge cases...\n'"'"');
  
  const uno = await createGenerator({
    presets: [presetWind4({ important: '"'"'#__nuxt'"'"' })]
  });
  
  // Test various utilities that use CSS variables
  const testCases = [
    '"'"'text-red-500'"'"',
    '"'"'text-red-500/50'"'"',
    '"'"'text-opacity-50'"'"',
    '"'"'bg-red-500'"'"',
    '"'"'bg-red-500/50'"'"',
    '"'"'bg-opacity-50'"'"',
    '"'"'border-red-500'"'"',
    '"'"'border-red-500/50'"'"',
    '"'"'border-opacity-50'"'"',
    '"'"'text-stroke-red-500'"'"',
    '"'"'text-stroke-opacity-50'"'"',
    '"'"'text-shadow-red-500'"'"',
    '"'"'text-shadow-opacity-50'"'"',
    '"'"'decoration-red-500'"'"',
    '"'"'underline-red-500'"'"'
  ];
  
  for (const utility of testCases) {
    const { css } = await uno.generate(utility);
    await checkCSSVariables(css, utility);
  }
  
  // Test multiple utilities together
  console.log('"'"'\n🧪 Testing multiple utilities together...'"'"');
  const { css: multiCss } = await uno.generate('"'"'text-red-500 bg-blue-500 border-green-500 text-opacity-75 bg-opacity-50'"'"');
  await checkCSSVariables(multiCss, '"'"'multiple utilities'"'"');
  
  console.log('"'"'\n✨ Edge case testing completed!'"'"');
}

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_final_validation.cjs --file_text 'const { createGenerator } = require('"'"'@unocss/core'"'"');
const { presetWind4 } = require('"'"'@unocss/preset-wind4'"'"');

async function validateCSS(css, testName) {
  console.log(`\n🔬 ${testName}`);
  
  // Check 1: @property rules should never be inside a selector
  const propertyRules = css.match(/@property\s+[^{]+\{[^}]+\}/g) || [];
  let hasInvalidPropertyRule = false;
  
  propertyRules.forEach((rule) => {
    // Check if the @property rule is incorrectly nested inside a selector
    const lines = css.split('"'"'\n'"'"');
    let propertyLineIndex = -1;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
      if (lines[i].trim() === rule.trim()) {
        propertyLineIndex = i;
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (propertyLineIndex > 0) {
      // Check the previous line to see if there'"'"'s a selector
      const previousLine = lines[propertyLineIndex - 1].trim();
      if (previousLine && !previousLine.startsWith('"'"'/*'"'"') && !previousLine.startsWith('"'"'@'"'"')) {
        // This means the @property rule is inside a selector block
        console.log(`❌ @property rule is inside selector: ${rule}`);
        hasInvalidPropertyRule = true;
        return;
      }
    }
    
    // Also check if the rule itself contains a selector before @property
    if (rule.match(/^[^{]*[.#\[]/)) {
      console.log(`❌ @property rule has selector prefix: ${rule}`);
      hasInvalidPropertyRule = true;
      return;
    }
  });
  
  if (!hasInvalidPropertyRule && propertyRules.length > 0) {
    console.log('"'"'✅ All @property rules are correctly positioned'"'"');
  }
  
  // Check 2: CSS variables should be properly defined and used
  const opacityVars = ['"'"'--un-text-opacity'"'"', '"'"'--un-bg-opacity'"'"', '"'"'--un-border-opacity'"'"'];
  let allVarsValid = true;
  
  opacityVars.forEach(varName => {
    const hasDefinition = css.includes(`${varName}:`);
    const hasPropertyRule = css.includes(`@property ${varName}`);
    const hasUsage = css.includes(`var(${varName})`);
    
    if (hasUsage && (!hasDefinition || !hasPropertyRule)) {
      console.log(`❌ ${varName}: used but not properly defined`);
      allVarsValid = false;
    } else if (hasDefinition && hasPropertyRule) {
      console.log(`✅ ${varName}: properly defined and managed`);
    }
  });
  
  return !hasInvalidPropertyRule && allVarsValid;
}

async function main() {
  console.log('"'"'🚀 Final validation of the @property rule fix\n'"'"');
  
  const testCases = [
    {
      name: '"'"'Original issue: important="#__nuxt"'"'"',
      config: { important: '"'"'#__nuxt'"'"' },
      utility: '"'"'text-red-500'"'"'
    },
    {
      name: '"'"'Multiple opacity variables'"'"',
      config: { important: '"'"'#__nuxt'"'"' },
      utility: '"'"'text-red-500 bg-blue-500 border-green-500 text-opacity-50'"'"'
    },
    {
      name: '"'"'Different important selector'"'"',
      config: { important: '"'"'#app'"'"' },
      utility: '"'"'text-blue-500'"'"'
    },
    {
      name: '"'"'Boolean important'"'"',
      config: { important: true },
      utility: '"'"'text-green-500'"'"'
    },
    {
      name: '"'"'No important option'"'"',
      config: {},
      utility: '"'"'text-purple-500'"'"'
    }
  ];
  
  let allTestsPassed = true;
  
  for (const testCase of testCases) {
    const uno = await createGenerator({
      presets: [presetWind4(testCase.config)]
    });
    
    const { css } = await uno.generate(testCase.utility);
    const isValid = await validateCSS(css, testCase.name);
    
    if (!isValid) {
      allTestsPassed = false;
      console.log('"'"'❌ Test failed'"'"');
    } else {
      console.log('"'"'✅ Test passed'"'"');
    }
  }
  
  console.log('"'"'\n'"'"' + '"'"'='"'"'.repeat(50));
  if (allTestsPassed) {
    console.log('"'"'✨ All tests passed! The fix is working correctly.'"'"');
    console.log('"'"'\n📋 Summary of the fix:'"'"');
    console.log('"'"'   - @property rules are no longer incorrectly wrapped with important selectors'"'"');
    console.log('"'"'   - CSS variables are properly defined and used'"'"');
    console.log('"'"'   - The important option works correctly for regular CSS rules'"'"');
    console.log('"'"'   - The original issue (--un-text-opacity being undefined) is resolved'"'"');
  } else {
    console.log('"'"'❌ Some tests failed. Please review the output above.'"'"');
  }
}

+  }
+  
+  // Check where the property definition is
+  const hasPropertyDef = css.includes('--un-text-opacity:100%;');

+  if (colorRule) {
+    console.log('\n💡 Found color-mix rule:');
+    colorRule.forEach(rule => console.log(rule));
+  }

+const { createGenerator } = require('@unocss/core');
+const { presetWind4 } = require('@unocss/preset-wind4');
+
+async function checkCSSVariables(css, utility) {
+  console.log(`\n🔍 Checking CSS for: ${utility}`);
+  
+  // Extract all @property rules
+  const propertyRules = css.match(/@property\s+([^{]+)\{([^}]+)\}/g) || [];
+  
+  if (propertyRules.length > 0) {
+    console.log('📋 Found @property rules:');
+    propertyRules.forEach((rule, i) => {
+      const isInsideSelector = rule.includes('#__nuxt');
+      console.log(`   ${i + 1}. ${isInsideSelector ? '❌ INSIDE #__nuxt' : '✅ Correctly placed'}: ${rule.trim()}`);
+    });
+  } else {
+    console.log('ℹ️ No @property rules found');
+  }
+  
+  // Check variable usage
+  const vars = ['--un-text-opacity', '--un-bg-opacity', '--un-border-opacity'];
+  vars.forEach(varName => {
+    const hasDefinition = css.includes(`${varName}:`);
+    const hasUsage = css.includes(`var(${varName})`);
+    
+    if (hasDefinition && hasUsage) {
+      console.log(`✅ ${varName}: defined and used correctly`);
+    } else if (hasDefinition && !hasUsage) {
+      console.log(`⚠️  ${varName}: defined but not used`);
+    } else if (!hasDefinition && hasUsage) {
+      console.log(`❌ ${varName}: used but NOT defined!`);
+    }
+  });
+}
+
+async function main() {
+  console.log('🧪 Testing edge cases...\n');
+  
+  const uno = await createGenerator({
+    presets: [presetWind4({ important: '#__nuxt' })]
+  });
+  
+  // Test various utilities that use CSS variables
+  const testCases = [
+    'text-red-500',
+    'text-red-500/50',
+    'text-opacity-50',
+    'bg-red-500',
+    'bg-red-500/50',
+    'bg-opacity-50',
+    'border-red-500',
+    'border-red-500/50',
+    'border-opacity-50',
+    'text-stroke-red-500',
+    'text-stroke-opacity-50',
+    'text-shadow-red-500',
+    'text-shadow-opacity-50',
+    'decoration-red-500',
+    'underline-red-500'
+  ];
+  
+  for (const utility of testCases) {
+    const { css } = await uno.generate(utility);
+    await checkCSSVariables(css, utility);
+  }
+  
+  // Test multiple utilities together
+  console.log('\n🧪 Testing multiple utilities together...');
+  const { css: multiCss } = await uno.generate('text-red-500 bg-blue-500 border-green-500 text-opacity-75 bg-opacity-50');
+  await checkCSSVariables(multiCss, 'multiple utilities');
+  
+  console.log('\n✨ Edge case testing completed!');
+}
+
+main().catch(console.error);

+const { createGenerator } = require('@unocss/core');
+const { presetWind4 } = require('@unocss/preset-wind4');
+
+async function validateCSS(css, testName) {
+  console.log(`\n🔬 ${testName}`);
+  
+  // Check 1: @property rules should never be inside a selector
+  const propertyRules = css.match(/@property\s+[^{]+\{[^}]+\}/g) || [];
+  let hasInvalidPropertyRule = false;
+  
+  propertyRules.forEach((rule) => {
+    // Check if the @property rule is incorrectly nested inside a selector
+    const lines = css.split('\n');
+    let propertyLineIndex = -1;
+    
+    for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
+      if (lines[i].trim() === rule.trim()) {
+        propertyLineIndex = i;
+        break;
+      }
+    }
+    
+    if (propertyLineIndex > 0) {
+      // Check the previous line to see if there's a selector
+      const previousLine = lines[propertyLineIndex - 1].trim();
+      if (previousLine && !previousLine.startsWith('/*') && !previousLine.startsWith('@')) {
+        // This means the @property rule is inside a selector block
+        console.log(`❌ @property rule is inside selector: ${rule}`);
+        hasInvalidPropertyRule = true;
+        return;
+      }
+    }
+    
+    // Also check if the rule itself contains a selector before @property
+    if (rule.match(/^[^{]*[.#\[]/)) {
+      console.log(`❌ @property rule has selector prefix: ${rule}`);
+      hasInvalidPropertyRule = true;
+      return;
+    }
+  });
+  
+  if (!hasInvalidPropertyRule && propertyRules.length > 0) {
+    console.log('✅ All @property rules are correctly positioned');
+  }
+  
+  // Check 2: CSS variables should be properly defined and used
+  const opacityVars = ['--un-text-opacity', '--un-bg-opacity', '--un-border-opacity'];
+  let allVarsValid = true;
+  
+  opacityVars.forEach(varName => {
+    const hasDefinition = css.includes(`${varName}:`);
+    const hasPropertyRule = css.includes(`@property ${varName}`);
+    const hasUsage = css.includes(`var(${varName})`);
+    
+    if (hasUsage && (!hasDefinition || !hasPropertyRule)) {
+      console.log(`❌ ${varName}: used but not properly defined`);
+      allVarsValid = false;
+    } else if (hasDefinition && hasPropertyRule) {
+      console.log(`✅ ${varName}: properly defined and managed`);
+    }
+  });
+  
+  return !hasInvalidPropertyRule && allVarsValid;
+}
+
+async function main() {
+  console.log('🚀 Final validation of the @property rule fix\n');
+  
+  const testCases = [
+    {
+      name: 'Original issue: important="#__nuxt"',
+      config: { important: '#__nuxt' },
+      utility: 'text-red-500'
+    },
+    {
+      name: 'Multiple opacity variables',
+      config: { important: '#__nuxt' },
+      utility: 'text-red-500 bg-blue-500 border-green-500 text-opacity-50'
+    },
+    {
+      name: 'Different important selector',
+      config: { important: '#app' },
+      utility: 'text-blue-500'
+    },
+    {
+      name: 'Boolean important',
+      config: { important: true },
+      utility: 'text-green-500'
+    },
+    {
+      name: 'No important option',
+      config: {},
+      utility: 'text-purple-500'
+    }
+  ];
+  
+  let allTestsPassed = true;
+  
+  for (const testCase of testCases) {
+    const uno = await createGenerator({
+      presets: [presetWind4(testCase.config)]
+    });
+    
+    const { css } = await uno.generate(testCase.utility);
+    const isValid = await validateCSS(css, testCase.name);
+    
+    if (!isValid) {
+      allTestsPassed = false;
+      console.log('❌ Test failed');
+    } else {
+      console.log('✅ Test passed');
+    }
+  }
+  
+  console.log('\n' + '='.repeat(50));
+  if (allTestsPassed) {
+    console.log('✨ All tests passed! The fix is working correctly.');
+    console.log('\n📋 Summary of the fix:');
+    console.log('   - @property rules are no longer incorrectly wrapped with important selectors');
+    console.log('   - CSS variables are properly defined and used');
+    console.log('   - The important option works correctly for regular CSS rules');
+    console.log('   - The original issue (--un-text-opacity being undefined) is resolved');
+  } else {
+    console.log('❌ Some tests failed. Please review the output above.');
+  }
+}
+
+main().catch(console.error);

+const { createGenerator } = require('@unocss/core');
+const { presetWind4 } = require('@unocss/preset-wind4');
+
+async function runTest(testName, config, utility) {
+  console.log(`\n🧪 ${testName}`);
+  
+  const uno = await createGenerator({
+    presets: [presetWind4(config)]
+  });
+
+  const { css } = await uno.generate(utility);
+  
+  // Check if @property rules are properly located
+  const propertyRules = css.match(/@property\s+[^{]+\{[^}]+\}/g) || [];
+  let hasInvalidPropertyRule = false;
+  
+  propertyRules.forEach(rule => {
+    if (rule.includes('#__nuxt')) {
+      console.log('❌ Found @property rule inside #__nuxt selector:', rule);
+      hasInvalidPropertyRule = true;
+    }
+  });
+  
+  if (!hasInvalidPropertyRule && propertyRules.length > 0) {
+    console.log('✅ @property rules are correctly positioned');
+  }
+  
+  // Check if CSS variables are properly defined and used
+  const usesColorMix = css.includes('color-mix');
+  const hasOpacityVar = css.includes('--un-text-opacity');
+  const usesOpacityVar = css.includes('var(--un-text-opacity)');
+  
+  if (usesColorMix && hasOpacityVar && usesOpacityVar) {
+    console.log('✅ CSS variables are properly defined and used');
+  } else {
+    console.log('❌ CSS variable issue:');
+    console.log('   - Uses color-mix:', usesColorMix);
+    console.log('   - Has opacity var:', hasOpacityVar);
+    console.log('   - Uses opacity var:', usesOpacityVar);
+  }
+}
+
+async function main() {
+  console.log('🚀 Running tests for @property rule fix...\n');
+  
+  // Test 1: Original issue - important: '#__nuxt' with text color
+  await runTest(
+    'Test 1: important="#__nuxt" with text-red-500',
+    { important: '#__nuxt' },
+    'text-red-500'
+  );
+  
+  // Test 2: Another important selector
+  await runTest(
+    'Test 2: important="#app" with text-blue-500',
+    { important: '#app' },
+    'text-blue-500'
+  );
+  
+  // Test 3: Boolean important
+  await runTest(
+    'Test 3: important=true with text-green-500',
+    { important: true },
+    'text-green-500'
+  );
+  
+  // Test 4: No important option
+  await runTest(
+    'Test 4: No important option with text-purple-500',
+    {},
+    'text-purple-500'
+  );
+  
+  // Test 5: Background colors with important
+  await runTest(
+    'Test 5: important="#__nuxt" with bg-red-500',
+    { important: '#__nuxt' },
+    'bg-red-500'
+  );
+  
+  // Test 6: Multiple utilities with opacity
+  await runTest(
+    'Test 6: important="#__nuxt" with multiple opacity utilities',
+    { important: '#__nuxt' },
+    'text-red-500 text-opacity-50'
+  );
+  
+  console.log('\n✨ All tests completed!');
+}
+
+main().catch(console.error);

+const { createGenerator } = require('@unocss/core');
+const { presetWind4 } = require('@unocss/preset-wind4');
+
+async function main() {
+  console.log('🧪 Testing important option with @property rules\n');
+  
+  // Test case 1: important = '#__nuxt' (original issue)
+  console.log('1. Testing important: \'#__nuxt\':');
+  const uno1 = await createGenerator({
+    presets: [presetWind4({ important: '#__nuxt' })]
+  });
+  
+  const { css: css1 } = await uno1.generate('text-red-500');
+  console.log('✅ Generated CSS includes:');
+  console.log('   - @property rule:', css1.includes('@property --un-text-opacity'));
+  console.log('   - Correct placement:', !css1.includes('#__nuxt @property'));
+  console.log('   - Color rule with #__nuxt:', css1.includes('#__nuxt :is(.text-red-500)'));
+  
+  // Test case 2: important = true
+  console.log('\n2. Testing important: true:');
+  const uno2 = await createGenerator({
+    presets: [presetWind4({ important: true })]
+  });
+  
+  const { css: css2 } = await uno2.generate('text-red-500');
+  console.log('✅ Generated CSS includes:');
+  console.log('   - @property rule:', css2.includes('@property --un-text-opacity'));
+  console.log('   - Color rule with !important:', css2.includes('!important'));
+  
+  // Test case 3: no important
+  console.log('\n3. Testing no important option:');
+  const uno3 = await createGenerator({
+    presets: [presetWind4()]
+  });
+  
+  const { css: css3 } = await uno3.generate('text-red-500');
+  console.log('✅ Generated CSS includes:');
+  console.log('   - @property rule:', css3.includes('@property --un-text-opacity'));
+  console.log('   - Normal CSS rules:', css3.includes('.text-red-500{'));
+  
+  console.log('\n✨ All tests passed! The fix correctly handles @property rules with important option.');
+}
+
+main().catch(console.error);
